prepared.module target=riscv64-linux-gnu route=semantic_bir_shared
completed_phases: legalize stack_layout liveness out_of_ssa regalloc
invariants:
  - no_target_facing_i1
  - no_phi_nodes
notes:
  - [prealloc] prealloc owns the shared semantic-BIR to prealloc-BIR route before MIR lowering
  - [legalize] bootstrap BIR legalize kept semantic CFG and phi form intact while promoting i1 values plus function signature/storage bookkeeping, memory-address/load-store bookkeeping, and call ABI metadata
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'topline' with 5 home slot(s) and 16 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'midline' with 7 home slot(s) and 16 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'botline' with 7 home slot(s) and 16 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'print_led' with 11 home slot(s) and 32 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout prepared function 'main' with 160 home slot(s) and 160 bytes of frame space
  - [stack_layout] stack layout now emits provisional stack objects, elides dead and copy-coalesced home slots, and only allocates frame storage for objects that still require dedicated homes
  - [liveness] liveness now computes BIR named-value intervals, exact def/use program points, predecessor-edge phi uses, call points, CFG-aware live-through extension, and loop depth independently of stack-layout object identity
  - [out_of_ssa] out_of_ssa removed phi nodes from live prepared BIR and published authoritative join-transfer plus parallel-copy obligations
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'topline' with 17 allocation constraint(s) and 57 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 4 register(s) and 13 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'midline' with 35 allocation constraint(s) and 184 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 5 register(s) and 30 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'botline' with 33 allocation constraint(s) and 168 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 5 register(s) and 28 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'print_led' with 316 allocation constraint(s) and 5559 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 35 register(s) and 281 stack slot(s)
  - [regalloc] regalloc seeded function 'main' with 3 allocation constraint(s) and 3 interference edge(s) from active liveness; assigned 3 register(s) and 0 stack slot(s)

  block block_87 terminator=branch target=for.latch.87
  block block_88 terminator=return

    incoming [tern.else.end.7] -> 0
    edge_transfer tern.then.end.5 -> tern.end.8 incoming=1 destination=%t9
    edge_transfer tern.else.end.7 -> tern.end.8 incoming=0 destination=%t9
